    [CreatedBy] uniqueidentifier NULL,
    [Created] AS GetUtcDate(),
    [ModifiedBy] uniqueidentifier NULL,
    [Modified] AS GetUtcDate(),
    [RecordStatusId] int NULL,
    [ProfileId] int NOT NULL,
    [JobTypeId] int NULL,
    [JobHour] decimal(3,2) NOT NULL,
    [ContractTypeId] int NULL,
    [ContractStartDate] Date NOT NULL,
    [ContractEndDate] Date NOT NULL,
    [CompanyName] nvarchar(100) NOT NULL,
    [VATNo] nvarchar(100) NULL,
    [LegalCompanyAddress] nvarchar(500) NULL,
    [OfficeAddress] nvarchar(500) NULL,
    [BranchAddress] nvarchar(500) NULL,
    [ChamberOfCommerceRegNo] nvarchar(100) NULL,
    [ChamberOfCommerceCityName] nvarchar(100) NULL,
    [REANo] nvarchar(100) NULL,
    [ATECONo] nvarchar(100) NULL,
    [SCIANo] nvarchar(100) NULL,
    [SCIACityName] nvarchar(100) NULL,
    [IsShareHolder] bit NULL,
    [PercentageOfShare] decimal(3,2) NOT NULL,
    [NotaioInfo] nvarchar(100) NULL,
    [CompanyRepresentative] nvarchar(100) NULL,
    CONSTRAINT [PK_ProfOccupationInfo] PRIMARY KEY ([OccupationInfoId]),
    CONSTRAINT [FK_ProfOccupationInfo_LU_ContractType_ContractTypeId] FOREIGN KEY ([ContractTypeId]) REFERENCES [LU_ContractType] ([ContractTypeId]) ON DELETE NO ACTION,
    CONSTRAINT [FK_ProfOccupationInfo_LU_JobType_JobTypeId] FOREIGN KEY ([JobTypeId]) REFERENCES [LU_JobType] ([JobTypeId]) ON DELETE NO ACTION,
    CONSTRAINT [FK_ProfOccupationInfo_ProfBasicInfos_ProfileId] FOREIGN KEY ([ProfileId]) REFERENCES [ProfBasicInfos] ([ProfileId]) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    CONSTRAINT [FK_ProfOccupationInfo_RecordStatus_RecordStatusId] FOREIGN KEY ([RecordStatusId]) REFERENCES [RecordStatus] ([RecordStatusId]) ON DELETE NO ACTION
);

    [WorkerInfoId] int NOT NULL IDENTITY,
    [CreatedBy] uniqueidentifier NULL,
    [Created] AS GetUtcDate(),
    [ModifiedBy] uniqueidentifier NULL,
    [Modified] AS GetUtcDate(),
    [RecordStatusId] int NULL,
    [ProfileId] int NOT NULL,
    [WorkerTypeId] int NULL,
    [Name] nvarchar(100) NOT NULL,
    [SurName] nvarchar(100) NOT NULL,
    [TaxCode] nvarchar(100) NOT NULL,
    [ContractNumber] nvarchar(100) NOT NULL,
    [MonthlySalary] decimal(8,2) NOT NULL,
    [StartDate] Date NOT NULL,
    [EndDate] Date NOT NULL,
    [Status] nvarchar(max) NULL,
    CONSTRAINT [PK_ProfWorkerInfos] PRIMARY KEY ([WorkerInfoId]),
    CONSTRAINT [FK_ProfWorkerInfos_ProfBasicInfos_ProfileId] FOREIGN KEY ([ProfileId]) REFERENCES [ProfBasicInfos] ([ProfileId]) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    CONSTRAINT [FK_ProfWorkerInfos_RecordStatus_RecordStatusId] FOREIGN KEY ([RecordStatusId]) REFERENCES [RecordStatus] ([RecordStatusId]) ON DELETE NO ACTION,
    CONSTRAINT [FK_ProfWorkerInfos_LU_WorkerType_WorkerTypeId] FOREIGN KEY ([WorkerTypeId]) REFERENCES [LU_WorkerType] ([WorkerTypeId]) ON DELETE NO ACTION
);
